   }

      function weightedRandom(cases) {
         var sum = 0;
         var min = 0;
         for(var key in cases) {
            chance = cases[key];
            sum += chance;
            cases[key] = {
               "chance": chance,
               "min": min,
               "max": min + chance
            };
            min += chance;
         }
         var testvariationInt = Math.random() * sum;
         for(var key in cases) {
            if(testvariationInt >= cases[key]["min"] && testvariationInt < cases[key]["max"]) {
               return key;
            }
         }
      }

function TsCcc(n, v, vendor, o) {
 if (!vendor)
  return false;
 o = o ? o : {};
 return __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents, success) {
  if (vendorConsents.grants[vendor] && vendorConsents.grants[vendor].vendorGrant) {
   document.cookie = n + '=' + (o.vne ? v : escape(v)) + (o.e ? '; expires=' + TmCED(o.e).toGMTString() : '') + (o.p ? '; path=' + o.p : '') + (o.d ? '; domain=' + o.d : '') + (o.s ? '; secure' : '');

    o.c();
    return true;

   });

}


/* TgCcc(): "getCookie consent conform(name, vendor, fallback)" */
function TgCcc(n, vendor, fallback) {
 var consentForVendor = false;
 __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents, success) {
  if (vendorConsents.grants[vendor] && vendorConsents.grants[vendor].vendorGrant) {
   consentForVendor = true;
  } else {
   consentForVendor = false;
  }
 });
 if (consentForVendor) {
  var c = document.cookie + ';',
   s = c.indexOf(n + '=');
  return s != -1 ? unescape(c.substring(s + n.length + 1, c.indexOf(';', s))) : null;
 } else {
  return fallback;
 }
}

  <script>
   function TsC(n,v,e,p,d,s,vne) {
 document.cookie = n+'='+(vne?v:escape(v))+(e?'; expires='+TmCED(e).toGMTString():'')+(p?'; path='+p:'')+(d?'; domain='+d:'')+(s?'; secure':'');
  return true;
}
function TgC(n) {
  var c=document.cookie+';', s=c.indexOf(n+'=');
  return s!=-1 ? unescape(c.substring(s+n.length+1,c.indexOf(';',s))) : null;
}

function __tcfapi_checkVendor(vendor, consentCallback, noConsentCallback) {
   function vendorConsented(vendor, consentCallback, noConsentCallback) {
      __tcfapi('getTCData', 2, function(tcData, success) {
         if(success) {
            if(tcData.vendor.consents[vendor]) {
               if(typeof consentCallback === 'function') consentCallback();
            } else {
               if(typeof noConsentCallback === 'function') noConsentCallback();
            }
         }
      }, [vendor]);
   }


   if(TgC('euconsent-v2')) {
      vendorConsented(vendor, consentCallback, noConsentCallback);
   } else {
      __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function(tcData, success) {
         if(tcData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete') {
            if(success) {
               vendorConsented(vendor, consentCallback, noConsentCallback);
            }
         }
      });
   }
}

  <script>
   function __tcfapi_checkCustomVendor(vendor, consentCallback, noConsentCallback) {
    if(typeof __tcfapi == 'function') {
        __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents, success) {
            if ( TgC('euconsent-v2') ) {
                if(vendorConsents.grants[vendor] && vendorConsents.grants[vendor].vendorGrant) {
                    if(typeof consentCallback === 'function')
                        consentCallback();
                } else {
                    if(typeof noConsentCallback === 'function')
                        noConsentCallback();
                }
            } else {
                __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function(tcData, success) {
                    if(tcData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete') {
                        console.log('Consent: EventListener triggered', tcData);
                        __tcfapi('getCustomVendorConsents', 2, function(vendorConsents, success) {
                            if(vendorConsents.grants[vendor] && vendorConsents.grants[vendor].vendorGrant) {
                                if(typeof consentCallback === 'function')
                                    consentCallback();
                            } else {
                                if(typeof noConsentCallback === 'function')
                                    noConsentCallback();
                            }
                        })
                    }
                });
            };
        });
    } else {
        if(typeof consentCallback === 'function') consentCallback();
    }
}

   /* Check and repair click tracking consent links */
 TClickTrackingCK = function(){ 
  this.init();
 }
TClickTrackingCK.prototype = {
  tpPending : [],
  consentIsLoaded : false,
  tcString : "",
  add : function(container) {

     if(this.consentIsLoaded) {
      this.checkConsentForTP(container);
     } else {

      this.tpPending.push(container);
     }
  },
  init : function() {

   let _t=this;

   __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function(tcData, success) {

     if(success && (["loaded"]).indexOf(tcData.cmpStatus) !== -1) {
     _t.consentIsLoaded = true;
     _t.tcString = tcData.tcString;
       for(var i = 0; i < _t.tpPending.length; i++) {

          _t.checkConsentForTP(_t.tpPending[i]);
       }
     }
   });
  },
  checkConsentForTP : function (container) {
    let _t=this;
    let hr=container.attr('href');

    if ( hr.indexOf('?') > -1 ) {
      if ( ( hr.indexOf('gdpr=') > -1 && hr.indexOf('gdpr_consent=') > -1 ) || ( hr.indexOf('gdpr%3D') > -1 && hr.indexOf('gdpr_consent%3D') > -1 ) ){
        if ( hr.indexOf('%24%7BGDPR%7D')>-1 ) {
          hr=hr.replace(/\%24\%7BGDPR\%7D/,1);
          hr=hr.replace(/\%24\%7BGDPR_CONSENT_\d+\%7D/,_t.tcString);

        }
        else if ( hr.indexOf('%gdpr%')>-1 ) {
          hr=hr.replace(/\%gdpr\%/,1);
          hr=hr.replace(/\%gdpr_consent_\d+\%/,_t.tcString);
        }

        else if ( hr.indexOf('${GDPR}')>-1 ) {
          hr=hr.replace(/\$\{GDPR\}/,1);
          hr=hr.replace(/\$\{GDPR_CONSENT_\d+\}/,_t.tcString);
        }
      } 
      else {
        let delim = hr.indexOf('?')>-1?'&':'?';
        hr += delim+'gdpr=1&gdpr_consent='+_t.tcString;
      };
    }
    else {
      hr += '?gdpr=1&gdpr_consent='+_t.tcString;
    };
    container.prop('href',hr);
  }
}

/* Check, repair and call view tracking consent links */

 TtrackingpixelCK = function(){  
  this.init();
 }
TtrackingpixelCK.prototype = {
  tpPending : [],
  consentIsLoaded : false,
  tcString : "",
  add : function( htmlcode, container ) {
     if(this.consentIsLoaded) {
      this.checkConsentForTP(htmlcode, container);
     } else {
      this.tpPending.push({htmlcode: htmlcode, container: container});
     }
  },
  init : function () {
   let _t=this;
   __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, function(tcData, success) {
     if(success && (["loaded"]).indexOf(tcData.cmpStatus) !== -1) {
     _t.consentIsLoaded = true;
     _t.tcString = tcData.tcString;
       for(var i = 0; i < _t.tpPending.length; i++) {
          _t.checkConsentForTP(_t.tpPending[i].htmlcode, _t.tpPending[i].container);
       }
     }
   });
  },
  checkConsentForTP : function (htmlcode, container) {
   if(htmlcode.match(/\$\{GDPR_CONSENT_\d+/g)) {
     htmlcode=htmlcode.replace( /\$\{GDPR\}/, 1 ); 
     htmlcode=htmlcode.replace( /\$\{GDPR_CONSENT_\d+}/, this.tcString );
   } 
   else if ( ! htmlcode.match(/gdpr\_consent\=/g) ) {
      // get the src part:
      let pre=htmlcode.substr(0,htmlcode.indexOf('src="'))+'src="';
      let src=htmlcode.substr(htmlcode.indexOf('src="')+5);
      let post=src.substr(src.indexOf('"')+1);
      src=src.substr(0,src.indexOf('"'));
      let delim = src.indexOf('?') > -1 ? '&' : '?';
      htmlcode = pre+src+delim+'gdpr=1&gdpr_consent='+this.tcString+post;

   }
   // in container ausgeben
   if(typeof container !== 'undefined' && container !== null) {
     T$(container).append(htmlcode);
   // am ende ausgeben
   } else {
     T$('body').append(htmlcode);
   }
   //console.log('gdpr replace',htmlcode);
  }
};

   var _smartWaiter = function (selector, callback) {
  function _requestFunction() {
    var _element = document.querySelector(selector);
    if(_element) {
      callback();
    } else if(document.readyState !== 'complete') {
      window.requestAnimationFrame(_requestFunction);

  }

}

  /*
 * perfMarksDealer - watches for rendering of containers with given CSS-Selector on the page and
 *                   sends a SpeedCurve performance Mark on rendering
 *                   to measure pageSpeed of single elements 
 *
 *  .add( markerId, selector ) - function that adds a container to be watched with
 *      markerId - the String that should be used to identify it in speedcurve
 *      selector - a CSS selector, which identifies the element to be watched
 *
 *  .watch() - the function that is subsequently called and holds the watchdog functionality
 *
 *  .start(timeout) - watchdog starts upon call of this function, when some of the elements
 *                    to be watched do not appear after given time the watchdog terminats
 *      timeout - an Integer represeting the number of ms after which the watchdog terminates
 *                default is 5000 (5s)
 */                  

var perfMarksDealer = {
  markerList:[],
  timeout:5000,
  startTS:0,
  add: function( markId, selector ) { 
    this.markerList.push( { 'markerId' : markId, 'selector': selector } );
  },
  watch: function() {
    var _this=perfMarksDealer;
    if (new Date().getTime() > _this.startTS + _this.timeout) return;
    var watchready=false;
    _this.markerList.forEach( function( el, idx ) {
      if ( T$(el.selector).length > 0 ) {
        performance.mark(el.markerId);
//        console.log("performance.mark",el.markerId);
        _this.markerList.splice(idx,1);
        if (_this.markerList.length == 0) watchready=true;
      }
    });
    if (!watchready) window.requestAnimationFrame(_this.watch);
  },
  start: function(t) {
    if ( t ) this.timeout = t;
    this.startTS=new Date().getTime();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(this.watch);
  },
};

// Start the watchdog
perfMarksDealer.start();
  </script>

/*
 * Lazyloading JS
 */
jsLazyLoadInit = function() {
  T.JSLL = {
     jslist : [],
     observer : new IntersectionObserver( function(e,o) {
                    T.JSLL.intersectCB(e,o); 
                  }, {
                    rootMargin: '100px'
                  }),
     isInitialized:false,
     init : function(options) {
       if ( T.JSLL.isInitialized ) return;
       T.JSLL.jslist.forEach( function(o,i) {
         T.JSLL.tObserve( o );
       });
       T.JSLL.isInitialized=true;
     },
     tObserve : function( o ) {
       var trg=document.querySelector(o.sel);
       trg.setAttribute('data-jsllid',o.num)
       T.JSLL.observer.observe(trg);
     },
     tUnobserve : function( o ) {
       var trg=document.querySelector(o.sel);
       trg.setAttribute('data-jsll-loaded',true)
       T.JSLL.observer.unobserve(trg);
     },
     addJS : function( selector, scriptsrc, callback ) {
       var jsline={sel:selector,src:scriptsrc,cb:callback,num:this.jslist.length};
       T.JSLL.jslist.push(jsline);
       if ( T.JSLL.isInitalized ) {
         T.JSLL.tObserve(jsline);
       }
     },
     intersectCB : function( e, obs ) {
       for ( i=0; i<e.length; i++ ) {
        var o= e[i];
        if ( o.isIntersecting ) {
          var ind = parseInt(o.target.dataset.jsllid);
          var llentry = T.JSLL.jslist[ind];
          var script = document.createElement("script")
          script.type = "text/javascript";
          script.onload = function() {
            if ( typeof llentry.cb === 'function' ) llentry.cb();
          };
          script.src = llentry.src;
          document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
          T.JSLL.tUnobserve(llentry)
        }
       }
     }
   };
};


domLazyLoadInit = function() {
 /* T-DOMLL 86357186 */



/*
 * Lazyloading DOM nodes
 *
 * to make a DOM node lazyloadable you need at least two things:
 *  - an anchor in the page, can be some container, just need to be catchable by a css-selector
 *  - a HTML document url to lazyload, should return pure HTML code
 *  - optional: a callback function which is executed, when the js is ready
 * Usage: you can add as much DOM nodes to lazyload as you want using the addNode function, 
 *   then call the init function when the containers you used are present in the DOM, 
 *   usually DOMContentLoaded
 *   from the time of initialization the added containers will be observed and loaded, 
 *   if/when visible
 * Trivia:
 *   - you can add DOM after initialization, the observation will start immediately
 *   - you can call init more than one time ( but you needn't ), it will not harm
 * Functions:
 *   - init() : has no options, starts observing container ID's
 *   - addNode( CSS-SELECTOR, URL, [CALLBACK] ) : add a DOM Node to be lazyloaded
 *      + CSS-SELECTOR : a valid css selector that has to deliver a DOM node when init() is called
 *      + URL : an url which when called delivers valid DOM node code which is inserted 
 *         into the container
 *      + CALLBACK : an optional function which is executed after the DOM node is loaded
 */

  T.DOMLL = {
     nodelist : [],
     observer : new IntersectionObserver( function(e,o) {
                    T.DOMLL.intersectCB(e,o);
                  }, {
                    rootMargin: '200px'
                  }),
     isInitialized:false,
     init : function(options) {
       if ( T.DOMLL.isInitialized ) return;
       T.DOMLL.nodelist.forEach( function(o,i) {
         T.DOMLL.tObserve( o );
       });
       T.DOMLL.isInitialized=true;
     },
     tObserve : function( o ) {
       var trg=document.querySelector(o.sel);
       trg.setAttribute('data-domllid',o.num)
       T.DOMLL.observer.observe(trg);
     },
     tUnobserve : function( o ) {
       var trg=document.querySelector(o.sel);
       trg.setAttribute('data-domll-loaded',true)
       T.DOMLL.observer.unobserve(trg);
     },
     addNode : function( selector, scriptsrc, callback ) {
       var jsline={sel:selector,src:scriptsrc,cb:callback,num:T.DOMLL.nodelist.length};
       T.DOMLL.nodelist.push(jsline);
       if ( T.DOMLL.isInitalized ) {
         T.DOMLL.tObserve(jsline);
       }
     },
     intersectCB : function( e, obs ) {
       for ( i=0; i<e.length; i++ ) {
        var o= e[i];
        if ( o.isIntersecting ) {
          var ind = parseInt(o.target.dataset.domllid);
          var llentry = T.DOMLL.nodelist[ind];
          var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
          var con=document.querySelector(llentry.sel);

          xhr.onreadystatechange = function (e) { 
            if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
              con.insertAdjacentHTML( 'beforeend', xhr.responseText );
              if ( typeof llentry.cb === 'function' ) llentry.cb();
            }
          }
          xhr.open("GET", llentry.src, true);
          xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'text/html');
          xhr.send();

          T.DOMLL.tUnobserve(llentry)
        }
       }
     }
   };





}

if ( typeof IntersectionObserver == 'undefined' ) {
  // IE does not know intersection observer, so we load the intersectionObserverPolyfill
  
  var script = document.createElement("script");
  script.type = "text/javascript";
  script.onload = function() {
    jsLazyLoadInit();
    domLazyLoadInit();
  };
  script.src = 'https://stats.t-online.de/intersectionobserverpolyfill-js/id_86294288/tid_js/index_ts386294288.js';
  document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);

}
else {
  jsLazyLoadInit();
  domLazyLoadInit();
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  if ( typeof T.JSLL === 'undefined' ) jsLazyLoadInit();
  T.JSLL.init();
  T.DOMLL.init();
});

    scrW:screen.width, scrH:screen.height, scrPR:W.devicePixelRatio||1,  /* Screen: Breite, Hoehe, Pixel-Faktor */

/* TsC(): "setCookie (name, value[, expire[, path[, domain[, secure[, valueNotEscape]]]]])" */

/* TgC(): "getCookie (name)" */
function TgC(n) {
  if(!N.cookieEnabled) return false;
  var c=D.cookie+';', s=c.indexOf(n+'=');
  return s!=-1 ? unescape(c.substring(s+n.length+1,c.indexOf(';',s))) : null;
}

/* TmCED(): Hilfsfunktion "make Cookie-Expire-Date (expire)" */
function TmCED(ex) {
  return typeof(ex)=='number' ? 
    //ex = ganze Zahl: relative Zeit in Sekunden
    new Date(TgT()+ex*1000) : 
    //ex = 'String':   absolute Zeit als Datum [+ optional Uhrzeit] 'JJJJ,MM,TT[,SS,mm,ss]' in normaler Schreibweise
    (ex=ex.split(',')).length==3 ? new Date(ex[0],ex[1]-1,ex[2]) : new Date(ex[0],ex[1]-1,ex[2],ex[3],ex[4],ex[5]);
}

// check localStorage support
function checkLocalStorage() {
  try {
    localStorage.setItem('test', 'test');
    localStorage.removeItem('test');
    return true;
  } catch(e) {
    return false;
  }
}

function changeCookieToLocalStorage(cookiename) {
  if ( !checkLocalStorage() ) {
    return TgC(cookiename);
  }
  if(localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != '' && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != null && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != 'null' && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != U) {
    return localStorage.getItem(cookiename);
  }
  var c = TgC(cookiename);
  eraseCookie(cookiename);
  return localStorage.setItem(cookiename, c);
}

// delete Cookie

  document.cookie = name+'=; Max-Age=-99999999;';  
}

/* Tinc(css_js [,attributes [,parent]]): Include von CSS / CSS-Datei / JS-Datei
*   css_js: CSS '.class1{color:#0f0} .class2{color:#eee}' / CSS-Datei.css '.../datei.css' o. '.../tid_css/...' / JS-Datei.js analog '.js' o. 'tid_js'

var _TclrI;
function TclrI(obj,va,vn) {
  if(typeof(va)=='number') switch(va) {
    case 1: va=obj.title; break;
    case-1: obj.av=obj.value; _TclrI=obj; setTimeout('TclrI(0,-9)',150); return;
    case-9: with(_TclrI) {if(av=='') value=title||''} return;
    case 2: var bi=T$(obj).css('background-image'); if(bi!='none') obj.bi=bi; obj.style.backgroundImage='none'; return; 
    case-2: if(obj.value==''&&obj.bi) obj.style.backgroundImage=obj.bi; return;
  }
  if(obj.value==va) obj.value=vn||'';
}

function TdateISO2Local(s,x) {
  var r;
  r = (r = /(\d+)-(\d+)-(\d+)T([\d:]+)\+([\d:]+)/.exec(s)) ? new Date(Date.parse(r[3]+' '+"MONjanfebmaraprmayjunjulaugsepoctnovdec".substr(r[2]*3,3)+' '+r[1]+' '+r[4]+' GMT')) : '';
  if(r&&x) {
    if(x>=1) r = "SoMoDiMiDoFrSa".substr(r.getDay()*2,2)+' '+Tz2(r.getDate())+'.'+Tz2(r.getMonth()+1)+'.'+ (x==1? r.getFullYear()+' | '+r.toLocaleTimeString().clrU200e().substr(0,5)+' Uhr' : '');
    else r = r.toLocaleString();
  }
  return !r||r=='NaN'?null:r;
}

/* ABC-Weiche 64568944.3 */
function TabcWeiche(ups,mck,ich) {
  if(ich && L.href!=ich) return 0;
  var c, i, n, p, u, z=Math.random()*100;
  if(mck) {
    n=mck[1]?mck[1]:'TabcW';
    if((c=TgC(n))!=null) {if(c<0) {TstatOK=0; L.replace(ups[-c-1][0])} return Number(c)}
  }
  for(i=p=u=0; i<ups.length; i++) if(z<(p+=ups[i][1])) {u=ups[i][0]; break}
  i++; c = u===0?0:u?-i:i;
  if(mck) TsC(n,c,mck[0]);
  if(u) {TstatOK=0; L.replace(u)}
  return c;
}

}

  /* spezielle/Einzel- Aufrufe */

}

/* TranslateChar 70268534.3 */

/* Funktion TTrsl8Char( s, map ) : translates in String s illegal Chars into legal Chars;
*   map = a map that assigns legal chars to illegal chars, of this form:
*   { 'x' : 'y', ... } where x is the illegal Char [string] and y is the legal Char [string] that replaces the illegal char
*   if parameter map is missing take the default map (see below)
*/
function TTrsl8Char( s, map ) {
  map = map || {'ö':'oe', 'ä':'ae', 'ü':'ue', 'Ö':'Oe', 'Ä':'Ae', 'Ü':'Ue', 'ß':'ss'};
  for(var i in map) if(s.indexOf(i)!=-1) s = s.replace( new RegExp(i,'g'), map[i] );
  return s;
}


/* Search/Query/Get-Parameter 72551414.8 */

/* TgSQ(x) - getSearchQuery/-GetParameter "URL?a=1&b=2&..." oder "URL?a=1;b=2;...";
* Parameter x = Aufrufart <-> Rückgabeart:
* x='[]'/nix: Array (a=2) / x='{}': Objekt (a=1) / x='Parameter-Name': P.-Wert (a=0)
*/
function TgSQ(x) {
  var sq=L.search.substr(1);  //Search-Query "?..."
  if(!sq) return false;  //keine Search-Query -> fertig
  var a= !x||x=='[]' ? 2 : x=='{}' ? 1 : 0;  //Aufrufart x <-> Rückgabeart a
  var t=sq.indexOf(';')!=-1 ? ';' : '&';  //Parameter-Trenner/Verbinder in URL ';' oder '&'
  if(a==0) {  //Parameter übergeben
    var r=new RegExp(x+'='+'(.*?)'+t);
    x=(sq+t).match(r);
    return x ? x[1] : null;  //Parameter gefunden / nicht gefunden -> zurückgeben / fertig
  }
  var nvp=sq.split(t), i;  //einzelne Name=Value-Paare der Search-Query als Array ['a=1', 'b=2', ...]
  for(i=0; i<nvp.length; i++) nvp[i]=nvp[i].split('=');  //als 2-dimensionales Array [[a,1], [b,2], ...]
  if(a==2) return nvp;  //Rückgabe als Array
  var nvo={};
  for(i=0; i<nvp.length; i++) {a=nvp[i]; nvo[a[0]]=a[1]}  //als Objekt {a:1, b:2, ...}
  return nvo;  //Rückgabe als Objekt
}

/* function TclrDopps(ps,c,ee) - Doppeleinträge löschen: Definition aus systemtechnischen Gründen in include-Statistik-ATI, nicht hier !!! */

/* TestKeksFa(cname) - Cookie-Test; cname=Cookie-(Basis-)Name:
* Funktionsweise: Durch Anhängen eines Query-Parameters an die URL werden 1...max.10 Session-Cookies einstellbarer Länge in der aktuellen Domäne erzeugt.
* Aufruf (mit cname=Cookie-(Basis-)Name, clen=Cookie-Länge):  "URL?cname=clen0,clen1,...,clen9"  ==>
*   ==> erzeugt Cookie0: 'cname0' mit clen0, Cookie1: 'cname1' mit clen1, ..., Cookie9 'cname9' mit clen9;
*   kommaseparierte Aufzählung der Cookie-Längen  ==>  entsprechend viele Cookies;
* Cookie-Namen: Cookie-(Basis-)Name + angehängte Ziffer 0...9;
* Cookie-Inhalt: entsprechend langer Ausschitt der Zeichenkette 'A123456789B123456789C123456789D123456789...';
* Cookie-Länge: vom Programm her begrenzt auf je 10000 B. Jeder Browser aber hat seine eigene Obergrenze, z.B.
*   aktueller Haus-Firefox "FrontMotion Firefox Nightly 28.0" = 4096 B; darüber wird kein Cookie mehr geschrieben!
*   Länge = Cookie-Gesamtlänge = Länge Cookie-Inhalt + Länge Cookie-Name
*   Länge 0 löscht einen Cookie
*   Länge all,100 schreibt alle Cookies mit Länge 100 B
*   Länge all,0 löscht alle Cookies
* Cookie-Expire: nicht gesetzt <-> Session-Cookie
* Cookie-Pfad & -Domäne: nicht gesetzt <-> aktueller Pfad & -Domäne
* 
* Beispiel:
* Der Cookie-(Basis-)Name im aktuellen Test ist 'TestCookie'; Aufrufe:
*   URL?TestCookie=1000  =>  schreibt Cookie 'TestCookie0' mit Gesamtlänge 1000 B (Inhalt = 1000 - 'TestCookie0'.length(=11) = 989 B)
*   URL?TestCookie=100,200  =>  schreibt Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (200B)
*   URL?TestCookie=0,500  =>  löscht 'TestCookie0' + schreibt 'TestCookie1' (500B)
*   URL?TestCookie=100,200,300  =>  schreibt Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (200B) + 'TestCookie2' (300B)
*   URL?TestCookie=all,100  =>  schreibt alle Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (100B) + ... + 'TestCookie9' (100B)
*   URL?TestCookie=all,0  =>  löscht alle Cookies 'TestCookie0' + 'TestCookie1' + ... + 'TestCookie9'
* 
*/
function TestKeksFa(cname) {
  var z='A123456789B123456789C123456789D123456789E123456789F123456789G123456789H123456789I123456789J123456789'; z=z+z; z=z+z+z+z+z;  //1000 Zeichen
  function TestKeksFi(cname,clen) {  //Cookie-Test (innen); Cookie-Name, Cookie-Länge
    if(clen==0) {TdC(cname); return 0}
    if(clen>10000) clen=10000;
    var x=Math.floor(clen/1000), i=0, c='';
    for(; i<x; i++) c+=z; c+=z.substr(0,clen%1000); c=c.substr(0,c.length-cname.length);
    TsC(cname,c);
    x=TgC(cname);
    return [cname, c.length, x?x.length:-1];
  }
  var x=TgSQ(cname);
  if(x) {
    x=x.split(',');
    if(x[0]=='all' && x[1]) {var n=x[1]; x=[n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n]}
    var len=x.length, i=0, n, cn, cl=[]; if(len>10) len=10;
    for(;i<len;i++) {
      n=Number(x[i]);
      cni=cname+i;
      if(isNaN(n)) {if(W.console) console.log('Parameterwert von '+cni+' ist keine Zahl!'); return -1}
      cl[i]=TestKeksFi(cni,n);
    }
    return cl;
  }
  else return -1;
}
